            <h3 class="d3-o-media-object__title">
             Cato's Coaching Calling: Former Colts LB Cato June Returns As A Coaching Intern During Minicamp
            </h3>
            <div class="d3-o-media-object__summary">
             <p>
              First Robert Mathis and then Reggie Wayne, and now, Cato June. The former Colts Pro Bowl linebacker is the latest former player on that 2006 Super Bowl XLI Championship team spending time in the off-season assisting Head Coach Frank Reich and his staff. June, the safeties coach at Howard University,  spent the last two weeks during organized team activities and minicamp as a part of the NFL's Bill Walsh Diversity Coaching Fellowship. He discusses his coaching passion with Colts.com radio host Matt Taylor and shares some fond memories during his time wearing the blue and white.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </a>

            <h3 class="d3-o-media-object__title">
             Film Study: Offensive Coordinator Nick Sirianni
            </h3>
            <div class="d3-o-media-object__summary">
             <p>
              Head Coach Frank Reich and Offensive Coordinator Nick Sirianni are installing a new offensive for the Colts this off-season. We’ve heard them describe it as “up-tempo”, using “multiple tight ends” and “dynamic running backs”, but what does all of that really mean? Colts reporter Caroline Cann sat in the film room with OC Sirianni to breakdown offensive concepts the you can expect to see from the Colts.
             </p>

      var disableOOP = false;
      if(!disableOOP){
        googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot(adUnit, 'oop').setTargeting('slot', 'oop').addService(googletag.pubads());
      }



      var modulePartnerCampaignID = '';
      if(modulePartnerCampaignID){
        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('partner', modulePartnerCampaignID);
      }

      var pagePartnerCampaignID = window.partnerCampaignID;
      if(pagePartnerCampaignID){
        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('partner', pagePartnerCampaignID);
      }

      var seriesName = '';
      if(seriesName){
        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('s3', seriesName);
      }

      googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();
      googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
      googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
      googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
      googletag.enableServices();

      if(googletag && googletag.pubadsReady){
        googletag.pubads().refresh();
      }
      else{
        window.requestAnimationFrame(awaitPub);
      }
    });

    function awaitPub(){
      var googletagFooter = googletag || {};
      googletagFooter.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];

      if(googletagFooter && googletagFooter.pubadsReady){
        googletagFooter.pubads().refresh();
        if(window.animationFrameIdAD){
          window.cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrameIdAD);
        }
      }
      else{
        window.animationFrameIdAD = window.requestAnimationFrame(awaitPub);
      }
    }
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
